mūrchanās tv ekaviṃśatiḥ punaḥ kīdṛśaiḥ mandrocceti mandraṃ nīcaiḥ uccam atiśāyitaṃ tāro yativiśeṣas tena paṭu spaṣṭaṃ yad gānaṃ tatparais tadāsaktaiḥ punaḥ kīdṛśaiḥ  viloleti vilolā yā dorvallarī vavādibhyo baliṃ dadyāt prayogas tu meṣavṛścikādhipataye maṅgalāya eṣa balir namaḥ evaṃ vṛṣatulādhipatayeśukrāya mithunakanyādhipataye budhāya karkaṭādhipataye candrāya siṃhādhipataye ātmanaḥ samarpaṇamantram āha ita ity ādinā svātmasamarpaṇe ity antena granthenaitaḥ pūrvaṃ prāṇabuddhidehadharmādhikārato jāgratsvapnasuṣuptyavasthāsu manasāvācā karmaṇā hastābhyāṃ padbhyām udareṇa KrdC atha śiṣya upoṣitaḥ prabhātekṛtanaityaḥ susitāmbaraḥ suveśaḥ dharaṇīdhanadhānyagokulairdhinuyād vipravarān hareḥ prasattyaiḥ  Krd athānantaram upoṣitaḥ kṛtopavāsaḥ śiṣyaḥ prabhāte prātaḥkāle Krd bhūyaḥ punar api pratarpya brāhmaṇān santoṣya punaḥ kathanam atyantatarpaṇārthaṃ parītyeti pāṭhe pradakṣiṇīkṛtyety arthaḥ deśikaṃ guruṃ praṇipatya namaskṛtya tasmai gurave dehine dehadhāriṇe Krd guḍasahitaṃ dadhi prātaḥkāle navanītasahitaṃ pāyasaṃ madhyāhne sasitopalam śarkarāvikārasahitaṃkṣīraṃ tṛtīyakāle ity amunā prakāreṇa dravyaṃ tarpaṇadravyaṃ kathitam  KrdC tarpaṇamantram catuḥsaptativāram ity amuṃpratarpayed yo nudinaṃ naro harim ananyadhīs tasya samastasampadaḥkare sthitā maṇḍalato bhivāñchitāḥ  Krd ity anena prakāreṇa prage prātaḥkāle catuḥsaptativāram amuṃ hariṃ kṛṣṇaṃ yo naronudinaṃ pratyaham ananyadhīḥ ekāgracittaḥ san santarpayet tasya puṃsaḥ maṇḍalataḥekonapañcāśaddivasāt arvāg iti tripāṭhinaḥ aṣṭacatvāriṃśaddivasābhyantara itilaghudīpikākāraḥ pañcatriṃśaddivasābhyantara iti rudradharaḥ abhivāñchitā ākāṅkṣitāḥ sakalasiddhisamṛddhayaḥ hastasthitā bhavanti atra sitopalāpuñjasya gaṇanā na kāryā  KrdC kāmyatarpaṇānantaram āhadhāroṣṇapakvapayasīdadhinavanīte ghṛtaṃ ca daugdhānnam matsyaṇḍīmadhvamṛtaṃ dvādaśaśaḥ tarpayen navabhir ebhiḥ  Krd  dhāroṣṇaṃ payaḥ tadānīntanam eva niṣpāditaṃ dugdhaṃ tathā pakvam payaḥ sādhitaṃ uddharativāgbhavaṃ mārabījaṃ ca kṛṣṇāya bhuvaneśvarī govindāya ramā gopījanavallabhaṅeśiraḥ  Krd vāgbhavam aim iti bījaṃ mārabījaṃ klīṃ kṛṣṇāyeti svarūpaṃ bhuvaneśvarībījaṃ hrīṃgovindāyeti svarūpaṃ abhinavāmbhojapatrābhanetram  Krd murāriṃ vande kīdṛśaṃ  kalpavṛkṣamūlāvasthite padmarāgamaṇighaṭite siṃhāsane upaviṣṭam punaḥ kīdṛśaṃ nīlābhaṃ śyāmaṃ tathā pītavastraṃ tathā hastapadme śobhamānau KrdC dadhibhakṣaṇaṅevahnijāyābhir aparo ṣtakaḥ suprasannātmane proktvā mama ity aparo ṣtakaḥ  Krd  caturthyanto dadhibhakṣaṇaśabdaḥ vahnijāyā svāhā etair varṇair aparo ṣtākṣaro mantraḥ suprasannātmane
